## Idea

The orbit of a point `x` for a permutation `f` is the set of point obtained by iterating `f` on `x`.

## Definition

### The groupoid of iterative orbits of an automorphism on a finite set

<pre class="Agda"><a id="6688" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6695" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6695" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="6699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6700" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6700" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6702" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6704" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4913" class="Function">𝔽</a><a id="6705" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6707" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6708" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6708" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="6710" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6712" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4952" class="Function">type-𝔽</a> <a id="6719" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6700" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6721" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="6723" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4952" class="Function">type-𝔽</a> <a id="6730" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6700" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6731" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="6735" class="Keyword">where</a>
  
  <a id="6746" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6746" class="Function">iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="6784" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6786" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6787" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6787" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6789" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6789" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6791" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6793" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4952" class="Function">type-𝔽</a> <a id="6800" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6700" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6801" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6803" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6805" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="6808" href="Agda.Primitive.html#764" class="Primitive">lzero</a>
  <a id="6816" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6746" class="Function">iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="6854" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6854" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6856" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6856" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6858" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="6864" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="6866" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="6868" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="6871" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6871" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="6873" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6875" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1767" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="6878" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6879" href="foundation.iterating-functions.html#1798" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="6887" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6871" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="6889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6890" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="6900" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6708" class="Bound">e</a><a id="6901" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6903" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6854" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6904" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6906" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6856" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6907" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="6912" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6912" class="Function">nat-iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="6954" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="6960" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6961" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6961" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6963" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6963" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6965" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6967" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4952" class="Function">type-𝔽</a> <a id="6974" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6700" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6975" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6977" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6978" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6978" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6980" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6982" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6746" class="Function">iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7020" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6961" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7022" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6963" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7023" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7025" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7027" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="7031" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6912" class="Function">nat-iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7073" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7073" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7075" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7075" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7077" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7079" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a>

  <a id="7086" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7086" class="Function">id-iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7127" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="7133" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7134" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7134" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7136" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7138" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4952" class="Function">type-𝔽</a> <a id="7145" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6700" class="Bound">X</a><a id="7146" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7148" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7150" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6746" class="Function">iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7188" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7134" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7190" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7134" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="7249" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="7253" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7254" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7086" class="Function">id-iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7295" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7295" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7296" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7298" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7300" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1820" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

  <a id="7308" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7308" class="Function">comp-iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7351" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="7357" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7358" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7358" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7360" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7360" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7362" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7362" class="Bound">z</a> <a id="7364" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7366" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4952" class="Function">type-𝔽</a> <a id="7373" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6700" class="Bound">X</a><a id="7374" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7376" class="Symbol">→</a>

    <a id="7430" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6746" class="Function">iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7468" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7358" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7470" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7360" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7472" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="7478" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6746" class="Function">iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7516" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7358" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7518" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7362" class="Bound">z</a>

    <a id="7599" href="elementary-number-theory.addition-natural-numbers.html#1164" class="Function">add-ℕ</a> <a id="7605" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7576" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="7607" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7587" class="Bound">m</a>
  <a id="7611" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="7615" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7616" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7308" class="Function">comp-iso-iterative-groupoid-automorphism-𝔽</a> <a id="7659" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7660" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="7665" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7665" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="7667" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7667" class="Bound">q</a><a id="7668" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7670" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7671" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="7676" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7676" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="7678" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7678" class="Bound">p</a><a id="7679" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="7682" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="7688" href="foundation.iterating-functions.html#2673" class="Function">iterate-add-ℕ</a> <a id="7702" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7665" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="7704" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7676" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="7706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7707" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="7717" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6708" class="Bound">e</a><a id="7718" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7720" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="7722" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="7724" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7725" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="7728" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7729" href="foundation.iterating-functions.html#1798" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="7737" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7665" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="7739" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7740" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="7750" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#6708" class="Bound">e</a><a id="7751" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="7754" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7678" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="7756" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="7758" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7667" class="Bound">q</a><a id="7759" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The equivalence classes of iterative orbits of an automorphism on a finite set

## Properties

### For type equipped with a counting, orbits of permutations are finite

<pre class="Agda"><a id="7947" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="7954" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7954" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="7958" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7959" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7959" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="7961" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7963" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="7968" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7970" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7971" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7971" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="7973" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7975" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#235" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="7978" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7959" class="Bound">l</a><a id="7979" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7982" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7982" class="Bound">eX</a> <a id="7985" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7987" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#1901" class="Function">count</a> <a id="7993" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7971" class="Bound">X</a><a id="7994" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7996" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7997" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7997" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="7999" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8001" href="foundation.automorphisms.html#1297" class="Function">Aut</a> <a id="8005" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7971" class="Bound">X</a><a id="8006" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8008" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8009" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#8009" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8011" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8013" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7971" class="Bound">X</a><a id="8014" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="8018" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="8027" class="Comment">-- The map `i ↦ eⁱ a` repeats itself</a>
  
  <a id="8069" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#8069" class="Function">repetition-iterate-automorphism-Fin</a> <a id="8105" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="8111" href="foundation.repetitions.html#1074" class="Function">repetition</a>

        <a id="8191" href="foundation.iterating-functions.html#1798" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="8199" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8200" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#6240" class="Function">nat-Fin</a> <a id="8208" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8209" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8216" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8217" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#2029" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="8242" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7982" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="8244" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="8247" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#8133" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8248" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8250" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8251" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="8261" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7997" class="Bound">f</a><a id="8262" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8264" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#8009" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8265" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="8311" href="univalent-combinatorics.pigeonhole-principle.html#9580" class="Function">repetition-le-count</a>

      <a id="8603" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8605" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1492" class="InductiveConstructor">succ-ℕ</a> <a id="8612" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8613" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#2029" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="8638" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7982" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="8640" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="8649" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="8651" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="8655" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8656" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="8660" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#8069" class="Function">repetition-iterate-automorphism-Fin</a><a id="8695" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="8701" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#8701" class="Function">point2-iterate-ℕ</a> <a id="8718" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8720" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="8724" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#8701" class="Function">point2-iterate-ℕ</a> <a id="8741" class="Symbol">=</a>

      <a id="18738" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18740" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="18746" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#18707" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="18748" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18749" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="18753" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#17209" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation</a><a id="18782" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="18791" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18793" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="18797" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#17209" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation</a><a id="18826" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="18834" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18836" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="18846" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7997" class="Bound">f</a><a id="18847" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="18855" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18857" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#8009" class="Bound">a</a><a id="18858" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18861" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
    <a id="18867" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18869" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18871" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a>
        <a id="18882" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18884" href="foundation.iterating-functions.html#1798" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="18892" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18893" href="elementary-number-theory.multiplication-natural-numbers.html#1358" class="Function">mul-ℕ</a> <a id="18899" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#18707" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="18901" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18902" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="18906" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#17209" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation</a><a id="18935" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18939" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="18949" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#7997" class="Bound">f</a><a id="18950" class="Symbol">))</a>
        <a id="18961" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18963" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="18967" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18968" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#617" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="18972" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#17209" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation</a><a id="19001" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="19005" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
      <a id="19013" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19015" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#18479" class="Function">mult-has-finite-orbits-permutation</a> <a id="19050" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#18707" class="Bound">k</a><a id="19051" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>      
### For finite types, the number of orbits-permutation of a permutation is finite.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="19157" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="19164" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19164" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="19168" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19169" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19169" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="19171" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19173" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="19178" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19180" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19181" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19181" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="19183" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19185" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="19186" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19188" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19189" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19189" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19191" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19193" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5425" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="19206" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19169" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="19208" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19181" class="Bound">n</a><a id="19209" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19211" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19212" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19212" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="19214" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19216" href="foundation.automorphisms.html#1297" class="Function">Aut</a> <a id="19220" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19221" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5520" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="19239" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19181" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="19241" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19189" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19242" class="Symbol">))</a>

                <a id="19910" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19912" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19914" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="19917" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19918" href="foundation.iterating-functions.html#1798" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="19926" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19927" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="19931" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19932" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#20702" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="19938" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19807" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="19940" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19646" class="Bound">k</a><a id="19941" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19944" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19945" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="19955" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19212" class="Bound">f</a><a id="19956" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19959" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19960" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="19964" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19648" class="Bound">p</a><a id="19965" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19968" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
                  <a id="19988" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19990" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19992" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2729" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="19996" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19997" href="foundation.iterating-functions.html#2673" class="Function">iterate-add-ℕ</a> <a id="20011" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20012" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="20016" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20017" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#20702" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="20023" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19807" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="20025" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19646" class="Bound">k</a><a id="20026" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20029" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19646" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="20031" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20032" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="20042" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19212" class="Bound">f</a><a id="20043" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20045" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19527" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20046" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20049" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a>

                        <a id="20380" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20382" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19527" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20383" class="Symbol">)</a>
                        <a id="20409" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20411" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19646" class="Bound">k</a><a id="20412" class="Symbol">))))))))</a>
    <a id="20425" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="20435" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#20435" class="Function">has-finite-orbits-permutation-a</a> <a id="20467" class="Symbol">:</a>
      <a id="20475" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20476" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#20476" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="20478" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20480" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2523" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="20484" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19181" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="20486" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="20488" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5520" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="20506" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19181" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="20508" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19189" class="Bound">X</a><a id="20509" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20511" class="Symbol">→</a>
      <a id="20519" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="20521" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="20523" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="20526" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#20526" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="20528" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20530" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20531" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1939" class="Function">is-nonzero-ℕ</a> <a id="20544" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#20526" class="Bound">l</a><a id="20545" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20547" href="foundation-core.cartesian-product-types.html#590" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="20549" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#1767" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="20552" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20553" href="foundation.iterating-functions.html#1798" class="Function">iterate</a> <a id="20561" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#20526" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="20563" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20564" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1821" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="20574" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19212" class="Bound">f</a><a id="20575" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20577" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19527" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20578" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20580" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19527" class="Bound">a</a><a id="20581" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="44577" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#44577" class="Function">coprod-sim-Eq-Rel-a-b-Prop</a> <a id="44604" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44606" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44607" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#44607" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="44609" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44611" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#28150" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="44613" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="44615" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#28150" class="Bound">X</a><a id="44616" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="44618" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="44624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44625" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#44625" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="44627" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="44629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44630" href="foundation.equivalence-relations.html#1187" class="Function">sim-Eq-Rel</a> <a id="44641" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44642" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#19257" class="Function">same-orbits-permutation</a> <a id="44666" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44667" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#2029" class="Function">number-of-elements-count</a> <a id="44692" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#28162" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="44694" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="44696" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44697" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="44702" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#28150" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="44704" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44705" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2132" class="Function">unit-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="44721" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44722" href="univalent-combinatorics.counting.html#2098" class="Function">equiv-count</a> <a id="44734" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#28162" class="Bound">eX</a><a id="44736" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="44740" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#44607" class="Bound">g</a><a id="44741" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="44743" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#28177" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="44745" href="finite-group-theory.orbits-permutations.html#28179" class="Bound">b</a><a id="44746" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="44749" class="Symbol">→</a>

    <a id="44817" href="foundation.coproduct-types.html#6146" class="Function">coprod-Prop</a>
